 ab wo mahila insaaf ke liye dar-dar bhatak rahi he

 mahila ne pradhanmantri modi se madad kii guhaar lagaai he
 40-year-old Laika, a resident of Jaipur, is a mother of two
 uskaa pati afjal property vyavsaayee he, jise sharaab kii lat he

 is dauraan lika kaa pati afjal jue main shart haar gaya

 baad main lika ko pataa chalaa ki ve kaagaj darasaltalaakanamathe
